# #############################################
# The default format for Han-Viet databases is as follows:
#     - first column:  Han character(s)
#     - second column: Vietnamese pronunciation
# But the format of this file is reversed.   So we need
# the following tag for WinVNKey to parse correctly:
#
# @First-column-is-pronunciation
